	Type: Written

Page 0:              Woodenaxe
             - The Law -
                  2014

     This book contains all
      information a player
       would need to know
         whilst playing on
          The Woodenaxe
        Adults only server

Page 1:                Contents

1:   Rules
2:  Conventions
7:  How to join
8:  FAQs


            PVP = WEST
    NON PVP =  EAST
Page 2:                   Rules

1:  No Griefing. Applies to
    every block placed by a
    player.
2: No Client Mods. If they
   affect the server they are    not allowed here
3: No Advertising/spam.
   Please take it elsewhere
Page 3:             Conventions

Use Common Sence.

Ask to build near others.

Unlocked containers are
free to loot.

Lock your chests.

Claim land with physical fences or a residence.
Page 4:             Conventions

Dont AFK for extended periods of time. 15 mins then you get kicked.

Dont run high frequency clocks. Matt will find them and remove them.

Keep farms to Reasonable
amounts.
Page 5:             Conventions

Read the Forums for how to's on "Residence" and
"Lockette". There are lots of posts by players that describe how to set up and modify protection for your blocks

If not there... Google
Page 6:             How To Join

1. Go To: Woodenaxe.com
2. Sign up on our forums.
3. Make a post in the 
   "New Members" section.
4.Include AGE, In Game 
   Name and a bit about 
   Yourself.
5. Wait, Matt will/will not
   accept you within 24h.
Page 7:                   FAQs

Someone killed my animals.
Can they be banned? No Animals are not loggable.
Protect your animals with a residence that has "butcher" set to false. Or box your animals in completely.

Page 8: Someone is being rude, can they be banned? No, You're both adults, Deal with it.

What IS considered harrasment:
- Spamming /tpa [player]
- Spawn killing in their 
  home
- Creating a res over their 
  Buildings
- Repeated killing in the
  East
Page 9: I teleported to a residence but it was a fall trap, it stole my stuff. Can they be banned? No, a fall trap is not against the rules, even in the east.
Generally ask before teleporting to an unknown resedence.
Try Asking for your stuff back nicely....
Page 10: If all else fails... go to the forums and create drama for us to be entertained.

------------------------------------Chunk [28, 7] Inside Chest at (-7734 63 -5510) r.-16.-11.mca------------------------------------
	Title: IKEA Igloo
	Author: kireinafujin
	Type: Written

Page 0: IKEA Igloo instructions. Your igloo will be 7x7x5. Follow the instructions below. The diagram in the box will help you along.

You will start by making a circle. 3 blocks for all four sides with a single block connecting diagonally.
Page 1: Top View, Bottom Layer

     SSS
   S     S
 S         S
 S    F    S
 S         S
   S     S
     S S

Repeat for second layer.
Page 2: In the center dig down 2, drop a nether block and light on fire to create the fire pit. Be sure your floor is not flamable.


-------------->
Page 3: Third Layer. Bring in one block and connect corners.

     ---
   - SSS -
 - S S S S -
 - S      S -
 - S S S S -
   - SSS -
     - -
Page 4: Fourth Layer. Fill in the four outside spaces.

     ---
   - --- -
 - - -S- - -
 - - S S - -
 - - -S- - -
   - --- -
     - -
Page 5: Fifth Layer. Place the last block center-top.

     ---
   - --- -
 - - --- - -
 - - -S- - -
 - - --- - -
   - --- -
     - -

	Title: Castle Black
	Author: supersnaketate
	Type: Written

Page 0:       §L   CASTLE BLACK


IN the Information age a castle was concieved, a castle of epic proportions. The castle lay atop a singluar peak surrounded by lakes of lava with boulder sized stepping stones afloat on the surface.
Page 1: The castle which can be clearly seen on the map lies in the east region of the world, its scorched  earth surroundings go out for miles. the flora and fauna have all but dissapeared and a lone path is the only lead to discovering the castle while on foot.
Page 2: Of the inhabitants, no one has truely been seen within its dark stone encrusted walls. Some claim to have seen a lone stranger wandering the castle, of which whom was rumored to have built it, this has never been proven.

     This book contains all
      information a player
      would need to know
        whilst playing on
          The Woodenaxe

Page 1:               Contents:

3:   Rules
5:   Non Official Rules
7:   How to Join
8:   FAQs
12:  Conventions
15:  Lockette
19:  Residence
22: Credits
Page 2:                  Rules:

A) NO GRIEFING
    Applies to every block a       player has placed or
    claimed

B) NO CLIENT MODS
    *Exceptions include:
     Optifine, Shaders,
     Minimaps.
     If it pings the server it
     is a no-no
Page 3:                  Rules:

C) NO ADVERTISING
    We dont want to know
    about your servers,
    telemarketer deals or
    Ebay items.

D) NO SPAMMING

E) WEST IS PVP
     Keep player killing
     in the west.
Page 4:        Non Official Rules:

A) KEEP YOUR DISTANCE
     About 300 blocks is the
     reccomended distance
     between you and
     someone else's builds

     *Exceptions can include
     Community builds
Page 5:        Non Official Rules:

B) DONT OVERLOAD THE
     SERVER
    Lots of mobs, Large
    redstone contraptions
    with fast clocks and
    selecting large
    residences you arent in
    will lag the server.
Page 6:             How to Join:

1:  Sign up on our forums
    forum.woodenaxe.com
2: Post an introduction
    application in the
   "New Members" section
    Include your in-game
    name, age and any past 
    bans you may have
3: Wait for approval
Page 7:                  FAQs

A) Can someone be banned
    for killing my animals?
    No, Matt has deemed
    animals as non-loggable
    thus dont count as grief

    *animals may be culled
     by matt if you breed
     an excessive amount
Page 8:                  FAQs

B) Someone is being rude/
    vulgar to me, can they
    be removed?
    No, you're both adults,
    sort it out like adults.

    *if you dont like drama
     keep to yourself.
Page 9:                  FAQs

C) I teleported into a fall
    trap, i want my stuff
    back...
   always think smart when
   teleporting to unknown
   residences, store all
   your valubles/items
   before teleporting.
   
Page 10:                  FAQs

C) *ask nicely for your
      stuff back, you may
      just get it back.
      If not, unfortunatly
      fall traps are not
      against the rules, thus
      they do not require to
      give your stuff back.
Page 11:             Conventions:

A) Use common sense
B) Ask to build near others
C) Unlocked Containers
     are free to loot
    i) unless they are item
       frames inside a
       residence
    *"The Leopody incedent"
Page 12:             Conventions:

D) Lock your chests
E) Lock your doors
F) Hide yo kids!
G) You can claim land with
    blocks, as long as its
    clearly marked as
    claimed land.
H) AFK timer will kick you
    after 15 minutes of
    inactivity.
Page 13:             Conventions:

I) Dont become a
   multi-millionaire, people
   will hate you
J) Dont give a shit about
    people hating you
L) Respect Community
    Builds

Page 14:                Lockette:

Lockette is used to protect
all your containers, it can also be used to lock doors

1: Shift right-click a sign
   onto a chest or the block      above a door
2: type on the first line
              [private]

Page 15:                Lockette:

3: the second line will auto
    fill your name
4: that container/door is
    now only openable by
    you!

    * Add other people's
      names to the third and
      fourth line to allow
      them to access it too
     
Page 16:                Lockette:

    * For doors add:
               [timer:2]
       To the third or fourth
       line for a short timer
       that will auto close the         the door after you've
       opened it


Page 17:                Lockette:

    * Add:
               [everyone]
       To the third or fourth
       line to allow everyone
       to access it
 
    * One sign will work for
       opening a double door
       and iron doors
Page 18:               Residence:

Residence is used to protect your blocks/land/chests etc. 
1: Grab a wooden hoe
2: Select two corners of an
   area (including height)
3: /res select size
   will give you the size
   and price
Page 19:               Residence:

4: /bal
    to see how much money
    you have
5: /res create [resname]
   [resname] = a name you
   choose for the residence
6: If it created
    successfully then you
    now have protected land
       
Page 20:               Residence:

Use /res tp [resname] to
teleport to your res.

For more Information, and indepth tutorials on residence have a look in our forums "Help and HOWTOs" section
Page 21:                 Credits:

         Matt "Mdrollette"
            Server Admin

          Supersnaketate

	Title: The Nether
	Author: supersnaketate
	Type: Written

Page 0:     The Eternally Dammed 
  A Study of the Creatures
      Found in the Nether

                  2013
         SuperSnakeTate



Page 1: I first entered the nether with childishness. it was a very suprising world comprised of what i belive to be the minced meat of the damned souls whom have died.

It was no shock that this place with-held strange creatures the like of which ive never seen.
Page 2: I started my studies on the most common of creatures found here; The Zombie Pigman.

The anatomy of this creature resembles a very strong bi-pedal man with the colouring and form of a common pig. most if not all have the ability to use tools.
Page 3: They carry a golden sword, sometimes enchated; of which they smite they're foes.

Hunting in packs these creatures can get very aggressive and it is not wise to trigger they're defensive state.


Page 4: The Blaze is a race of sentient beings comprised of hardened glowstone rods, these rods often catch fire from their sheer compression levels, they are very good fuel.

The Blaze usually only summon around a central summoning block found on nether fortress
Page 5: Ghasts are the most feared of all creatures in the nether, their howling crys shock you to the very bone.

They shoot fireballs out their mouths which are extreemly explosive.
watch out!

they are very easy to kill with a bow an arrow and drop ghast tears
Page 6: Something i have only rarely found are The Magma Slimes/Cubes

much like the overworld equivilent, they come in varying sizes.

Not much to them other than they are guite hot and will burn on touch
Page 7: Wither Skeletons.
rare black skeletons weilding swords.

i know not much of these strange aboninations but of the secret to spawning the most feared creater of all

Collect three wither skelton heads and 4 soul sand. Combine them to make....
Page 8: The Wither.

information has yet to be collected.


Theorys suggest it created a beast trapped by the Endermen

	Title: Castle Black
	Author: supersnaketate
	Type: Written

Page 0:          CASTLE BLACK


IN the Information age a castle was concieved, a castle of epic proportions. The castle lay atop a singluar peak surrounded by lakes of lava with boulder sized stepping stones afloat on the surface.
Page 1: The castle which can be clearly seen on the map lies in the east region of the world, its scorched  earth surroundings go out for miles. the flora and fauna have all but dissapeared and a lone path is the only lead to discovering the castle while on foot.
Page 2: Of the inhabitants, no one has truely been seen within its dark stone encrusted walls. Some claim to have seen a lone stranger wandering the castle, of which whom was rumored to have built it, this has never been proven.

Page 0: ===================     LUCY BELL LANE
===================

Calico's most distinguished and long time resident was Lucy Bell Lane (1874-1967).

Known as the "Queen of Calico", Lucy lived at Calico for nearly 67 years.
Page 1: Of her many gifts, she is most remembered for her warm hospitality and vivid storytelling of the historic Calico silver camp.

Lucy was indeed part of the history of Calico and was an accomplished prospector.
Page 2: Lucy Bell King arrived at Calico with her parents, her two brothers and sister in 1884, three years after the initial discovery of silver.

In 1892 at the age of 18, she married John Lane. They bought a grocery store which briefly prospered
Page 3: but then quickly declined as a result of a slumping silver market. The Lanes left Calico in 1899 and returned for good in 1916, making the Lane's store building their home.

In 1920, the Lanes moved into the old courthouse & post office building, which
Page 4: would be Lucy's home until 1965.

John Lane died in 1934 & Lucy died in 1967 at the age of 93.

------------------------------------Chunk [9, 1] Inside Chest at (159 69 -2017) r.0.-4.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Eternal Lord
	Author: The_Samurai_Duke
	Type: Written

Page 0: The heroic deeds of the Eternal Lord. 

Birth.
Born to an empoverished noble family in the 447th year of The old Empire, The Eternal Lord seemed to have no notable traits, that is until the civil war...
Page 1: Imperial year 467.

Onset of war.

467 Imperial date.

Ortheus VII Succeeds the throne after the death of his father. Ortheus, the product of inbreeding, show signs of...illnesses
Page 2: Ortheus VII has been ruling for 4 years now. Most people relastively close to the Emperor are fully aware of his schizophrenia. The commoners are not sure, but many believe so. The Empire has waged more wars in the past 4 years than
Page 3: in the previous 40 years.The treasury has been depleted, food growing scarce and talk of a peasant rebellions to the north and an ethnic rebellion to the south. The Empire is nearing the brink of ruin. Various Lords and prominent figures..
Page 4: begin to talk. One of them is our Eternal Lord.
 
Our Eternal Lord, Wilhelm III, has risen to prominence as of late. Having successfully graduating top of his class in the Imperial Naval Academy and...
Page 5: his family having climbed it's way back up from financial ruin, thanks to his uncle's death allowing his father to take over the family as patriarch. Under Wilhem's father, the family managed to revive local industry and invest in more...
Page 6: infrastructure, a gamble at the time that would pay off big later on. He also expanded the reach of the Empire by colonizing new lands. Lands where his son Wilhem III would later move the family capital to and where he would be buried.
Page 7: Imperial Year 471

The start of war.

Ortheus, growing ever more insane, is furious. The gossip of the Lords and wealthy merchants has reached his ears. Ortheus begins a purge that would see 10,000 nobles,
Page 8: merchants, and commoners executed. Entire families eradicated and laws are put in place to make it illegal to speak lies against the Imperial family. 
The remaining figures powerful enough and bold enough to stand against Ortheus..
Page 9: meet one final time. During this convention the vast majority agree that somethng must be done, so they decide to support previous Emperor's nephew to be placed on the throne in a coup. 
His name was Artefic.
Page 10: Artefic, having the support of many of the nobility, addresses the Imperial Court. the Imperial court is mainly for show now, previously it was used as a legeslative body to act on decisions such as succession, war, and trade. The act
Page 11: would be no less symbolic though. 

In his address to the court Artefic condemned the new laws and resent executions as a black stain on the Empire's noble history. The Imperial Court, packed with Ortheus' side...
Page 12: was not moved, however the speech was heard around the Empire. Peasant to nobles had began to stand together against the Emperor with encouragement from the recent speech. Ortheus was silent, but swift. Sending a legion to arrest
Page 13: Artefic at his castle under the charges of spreading "lies" about the Imperial family. However, Artefic was already 2 steps ahead of his demented cousin had sent a spy into the Emperor's circle months ahead of the speech.
Page 14: Having already recieved information of the impending attack, Artefic called on his friend, our Lord, Wilhelm III to do the impossible. Defeat the invading force.
Wilhelm would have to move troops and supplies without notice of Imperial..
Page 15: forces in only a months time. The army sent by the Empire was 10,000 strong, and at best The Rebels could hope for 6,000 under supplied troops. Wilhelm would have many sleepless nights ahead. 
Page 16: Imperial Year 471

The first battle.

Having managed to pull off the seemingly possible Wilhelm managed to bring in 5,500 troops, get defensive fortifications built in the forests and supply the castle..
Page 17: Wilhelm knew he couldn't defeat the well trained, well supplied Empire head on so he devised a plan to strike them with a small force in the forests ahead of the castle. Enough to thin their ranks some, but not enough to alert them to a larger 
Page 18: force in the castle.

Wilhelm's gorilla attacks in the forest thinned the Imperial forces from 10,000 to 9,553, using only small scouting parties and well placed traps through the forest. Less than what was hoped for Wilhelm  
Page 19: had to devise another plan, for Imperial forces would be on the castle in 3 days. 

Wilhelm thought of a genius plan that night while in the tavern. He would take all the alcohol in the castle and the villages nearby and stage
Page 20: a large shipment for the Imperial forces to capture. This was a risky plan, because he knew without that alcohol his weaker and non battle hardened troops would quickly lose nerve, but Wilhelm decided to make the gamble. 3 days later the Imperials
Page 21: reached the walls, where they quickly pillaged everything outside the walls, including the staged alcohol caravan near the gates. 
 
 Later that night Wilhelm snuck his troops out of the rear and side gates and charged the ...
Page 22: enemy camp. Wilhelm's plan worked perfectly. Not only were a large portion of Imperial forces drunk, but the security around the gates were relaxed aswell. That night was known as the begining of the end for the Imperials.
Page 23: Wilhelm then lead rebel forces on the same road the Imperials took towards the capital. Having assumed the legion would win, or at least not be utterly shattered so quickly. Defense in the capital was nothing but inexperienced militia.
Page 24: The Imperial Capital was quickly captured, however Ortheus would manage to escape. The war would drag on for another 3 years all across the Empire until 474 when Ortheus would take his own life during the final seige of his island fortress, Izo. 
Page 25: For his tremendous service for leading the Rebel forces as Supreme Commander of Rebel forces, Wilhelm was granted the title of Archduke and granted Independent member state of the Empire. Only 4 other leaders would be granted such an..
Page 26: honor in history. 

Wilhelm now 27 and the leader of his own nation, decided to move the capital to the colony where his father retired and died before the war. There among the mountains he would erect a castle and village which would soon
Page 27: bustle into the City we live in today.

------------------------------------Chunk [20, 6] Inside Chest at (842 64 -1431) r.1.-3.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Yellow WallPaper
	Author: VigilBushido
	Type: Written

Page 0: Its is very seldom that meree ordinary people like John and myself secure ancestral halls for the summer. A colonial mansion, a hereditary estate, I would say a haunted house, and reach the height of romantic felicity--but that would be asking too much of
Page 1: fate! Still I would proudly declare that there is something queer about it. Else, why should it be let so cheaply? And why have stood so long untenanted? John laughs at me, of course, but one expects that in marriage. John is practical in the extreme.
Page 2: He has no patience with faith, an intense horror of superstition , and he scoffs openly at any talk of things not to be felt and seen and put down in figures. John is a physician , and perhaps--(I would not say it to a living soul, of course, but this is 
Page 3: dead paper and great relief to my mind--) perhaps that is one reason I do not get well faster. You see he does not believe I am sick! And what can one do?  If a physician of high standing, and one's own husband, assures freinds and relatives that there is
Page 4: really nothing the matter with one but temporary nervous depression--a slight hysterical tendency--what is one to do? My brother is also a physician, and also of high standing, and he says the same thing. So I take phosphates or phosphites--whicheve
Page 5: it is, and tonics, and journeys, and air, and exercise, and am absolutely forbidden to "work" until I am well again. Personally, I disagree with their ideas. Personally, I believe that congenial work, with excitement and change would do me good. 
Page 6: But what is one to do? I did write for a while in spite of them; but it does exhaust me a good deal--having to be so sly about it, or else meet with heavy opposition. I sometimes fancy that in my condition if I had less opposition and more 
Page 7: society stimulus--but John says that very worst thing I can do is to think about my condition, and I confess it always makes me feel bad. So I will let it alone and talk about the house. The most beautiful place! It is quite alone, standing well back from
Page 8: the road, quite three miles from the village. It makes me think of English places that you read about, for there are hedges and walls and gates that lock, and lots of seperate little houses for the gardeners and people. There is a delicious garden! 
Page 9: I never saw such a garden--large and shady, full of box-bordered paths, and lined with long grape-covered arbors with seats under them. There were greenhouses, too, but they are all broken now. There was some legal trouble, I believe, something about the
Page 10: heirs and coheirs; anyhow, the place has been empty for years. That spoils my ghostlines, I am afraid, but I don't care--there is something strange about the house--I can feel it. I even said so to John one moonlight evening, but he said what I felt was a
Page 11: draught, and shut the window. I get unreasonably angry with John sometimes. I'm sure I never used to be so sensitive. I thinkit is due to this nervous condition. But John says if I feel so, I shall neglect proper self-control; so I take pains to control
Page 12: myself--before him, at least, and that makes me very tired. I don't like our room a bit. I wanted one downstairs that opened on the piazza and had roses all over the window, and such pretty old-fashioned chintz hangings! But John would not hear of it.
Page 13: He said there was only one window and not room for two beds, and no near room for him if he took another. He is very careful and loving, and hardly lets me stir without special direction. I have a schedule prescription for each hour in the day; he takes 
Page 14: all care from me, and so I feel basely ungrateful not to value it more. He said we came here solely on my account, that I was to have perfect rest and all the air I could get. "Your exercise depends on your strenght, my dear" said he, "and your food
Page 15: somewhat on your appetite; but air you can absorb all the time." SO we took the nursery at the top of the house. It is a big, airy room, the whole floor nearly, with windows that look all ways, and air and sunshine galor. It was nursery first and then
Page 16: playroom and gymnasium, I should judge; for the windows are barred for little children, and there are rings and things in the walls. The paint and paper look as if a boys' school had used it. It is stripped off--the paper--in great patches all around the 
Page 17: the head of my bed, about as far as I can reach, and in a great place on the other side of the room low down. I never saw a worse papers in my life.  One of those sprawling flamboyant patterns committing every artistic sin. It is dull enough to confuse
Page 18: the eyein the following, pronounced enough to constantly irritate and provoke study, and when you follow the lame uncertain curves for a little distance they suddenly commit suicide--plunge off at outrageous angles, destroy themselves in unheard of
Page 19: contradictions. The color is repellent, almost revolting; a smouldering unclean yellow, strangely faded by the slow -turning sunlight. It is a dull yet lurid orange in some places a sickly sulphur tint in others. NO wonder the children hated it! I should 
Page 20: hate it myself if I had to live in this room long. There comes John, and I must put this away,--he hates to have me write a word. 

------------------------------------Chunk [20, 6] Inside Chest at (842 64 -1431) r.1.-3.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Sun Child
	Author: VigilBushido
	Type: Written

Page 0: It was a muggy morning in the great city of Conquestadors. The morning stench of blood and rotting flesh awakens me. I arise quickly to see the sun meet me face to face. When all of a sudden, there is a group of 5 men standing about my body ready to 
Page 1: dismantle me limb from limb. I can see the hate in their eyes and their grips tighten around the leather wraps securely holding swords half the size of a bear. For what could they be so mad about to reach this point. Well I'll tell ya it was the point of 
Page 2: war that nobody ever thought was possible. The year was 2128 and the world was at a standstill as Casma the last surviving species of alien catastrophic invasion as a last resort for their own survival coaxed human rebels into an allegiance that would 
Page 3: benefit only the most grutesk survivors of the planet. Only the vile would survive to live among these aliens in rule of the world. So this they thought until, they met Sergie the smiter of lox giants & inventor of meta physical changing elixors by the
Page 4: thousands. His power left him alone standing. Now Sergie is faced with some infidels that just didn't bother believing the myths. I quickly dash my left foot back side step drop down and sweep the legs from under my oppenents and my leverage of stability 
Page 5: gains I propel a jab into ones liver as well and a keen shot to ther others kidney. Now its just time to show off as I grab my trousers & shirt, leaving the men groveling over the floor. The next thing I'm doing is bringing an elixir up before me to 
Page 6: endulge in this heavy toxin, i warn the men you better run.... This is not some ordinary fixer upper magic drink. This is my own concoction that has been so true, to have me as the only one rebellion left against an overwhelming force for everyone else. 
Page 7: When the elixir mixes into my bloodstream not only am i increasing stronger with every muscle contraction. The blows destroy the cartledge & shatter the bones of my oppenents. These men are men no longer, I feel satisfied knowing their death saves
Page 8: lives of those away safe in their homes. This world once was made true until the aliens only fueled a fire while humanity layed the logs at their feet for decades without even knowing they existed. Nuclear power plants became the headquarters, satelites
Page 9: remote housing of their ships own technology. As they watched and manipulated the information to feed into their will to land and have an accompaning force. They indeed found those souls willing to do these deeds for the lavish promises of positions with 
Page 10: power promised to by the aliens themselves. But, What you say of the survivors....they fell off the planet one by one. The ground was infected with goncollow a single cell virus that excretes its waste in the form of vapor. This vapor would alter the mind
Page 11: infect it with the thoughts of vivid scense of slaughter & abondonment. To twin the mind into a genocidal maniac. That's the point, when my research was done. Time to apply the theories, page after page of proofs as they clutter my mind night
Page 12: after night until the connections seen becomes embossed in my mind. Now I survive, now i take heid and pack my bags. This is just another day of mine, as i became the man with tools given to me only the gods could have placed in the right order. My will 
Page 13: here is not to change the world but simply offer a choice. These Casma have taken the choice from humanity. So I give it back using my power to create such power weapons & elixirs. These that range from the most simplest comb that removes the iniquities
Page 14: from the mind. I bring more with blades that weild powers of pursuasion. The slicing only increases the chance that an opponent might feel that choice to lay down gurgling in their stomache is the choice. We only can hope that out of 200 thousand maybe I 
Page 15: can help 2 have the strength to make a choice than reside in the hell of their mind that these Casma wish humanity to stay. This is about the time where, well normally the hero is awarded. Unfortunately that star has burned its last light many decades 
Page 16: ago. The only light that lies here is the one of fury. The one that divides the strong from the Casma controlled maniacs. Even in this small glimer of hope i find consolation for all my work. I search high and slash low as I walk these treacherous lands. 
Page 17: Somebody once told me to stay the coarse and never mind the landscape. I now understand the true meaning of such blinds being placed on ones sight. I've been walking for 8 miles now and have convoked around 8 hundred souls to test my wit. They have all
Page 18: met the power of my elixir to no avail. Not one single soul could i convince to see they even had a choice. When the day ends, I wrap myself in silk sheets lined with micro jumba bacteria to disguise me as the remains of just another dead victim. 
Page 19: My eyes shut to the sounds of metal wreckage in the far distance. There in the distance is the pro arena where the Casma hold all their main source of power. It is here I will lay down my life and reunited with my loved ones I've lost. As I approach, my
Page 20: I see a child laying near the gate. What could this child be doing here, how could it have survived ? The small child brings his feet up under him. I see that this child is starved and disease ridden. Purely death seeking this child is the Casmas statue, 
Page 21: I now realize why he's there. The only thing that can penetrate me. A child lay waste to my soul. 

The End. 
by VigilBushido

------------------------------------Chunk [20, 6] Inside Chest at (842 64 -1431) r.1.-3.mca------------------------------------
	Title: The New World :1
	Author: Mandasity
	Type: Written

Page 0: Introduction

Hey guys! Manda here :) Before you read this little short story I wrote for my friends and everyone in WA, you should probably be warned :P  I tried to write creatively in the past but couldn't keep my interest past a few pages.. might lose 
Page 1: interest with this too but I promise to try and finish what I started. I also haven't written anything to be read by anyone since school and college.. so my punctuation and grammar will probably be off but I assure you that it is at the very least
Page 2:  readable. lol it's not just chicken scratch. This scifi short was 'strongly' influenced by a short titled 'The Metamorphosis of Prime Intellect'  written by Roger Williams which is free to read on the author's site without any downloads or payments or 
Page 3: any bs.. just google it if you're interested and it should be the top link. If you do read it you'll notice that our stories have a ton of similarities.  "Why the hell should I read your 'not even' amateur version when the good stuff is online for free?" 
Page 4: you might be wondering. Well for one I don't see a reason why you can't read both :P. They're both free (no need to pirate, rmj!)  Second, you love me.. we both know this so don't deny it cause we both know that'd be a lie.  Third, I tried to go in a
Page 5: different direction than Mr. Williams did with his novel. Mr. Williams is a software programmer with more knowledge than me about computers and... programming.. and his work reflects that. His work is strongly influenced by Asimov's literature and concept
Page 6: of the 3 laws of robotics (remember Will Smith in iRobot? That.) I, on the other hand, am a typical nerd with nerdy interests like scifi/fantasy movies, books, and games so my influences are a bit different. My interests are broader and hopefully this 
Page 7: novel will reflect that. The last thing I'd like to say is I'll take on any criticism on my writing or the story itself. Like it.. hate it.. feel free to let me know! :)
Page 8: Chapter 1
Her name was Clara Anderson, and she was an amazing woman. Before she was thrust into the New World, like everybody else, she was considered exemplary. At a young age she learned about the bush from her loving parents ,  Ben and Angela.
Page 9: They taught her about the beauty of the natural world, how to survive it's harshness, and the responsibility to be it's steward. 

That was in the past.

Clara loved the camping trips she had with her parents. To her it was fun and exciting to
Page 10: experience everything head on and when adulthood slowly creeped into her life the wonder she held for the world didn't fade. She had stepped into her parents shoes in a sense and was very proud of her knowledge and donned the role of a protector, for not
Page 11: everyone saw the value of such a lifestyle and even worse, did everything in their power to ruin it. Humanity, as a whole, was more concerned with other things than silly trees or wild animals.

Clara was an overachiever. One
Page 12: would think that a person with a fiery passion would find their life lacking in other areas, but Clara didn't fit into that category. She was an excellent student, later earning a PhD in environmental geochemistry which afforded her a career working with
Page 13: what she loves.  She was always physically fit, excersizing in ways most people at the gym couldn't understand or chose not to.  She had learned how to defend herself at a young age from her father and continued that education through brazilian jiu-jitsu 
Page 14: so she very well knew the difference between sculpting a body for display, and raw functional strength. Clara had also been a socially outgoing person ; the fact that most men would find her fetching physically and mentally stimulating only cemented her 
Page 15: status on the social ladder. She was an alpha in every sense of the word. 

There was almost nothing left but anger now, anger and disgust for the Machine, the New World, and everything in it. The last century had even threatened her sanity
Page 16: but she refused to go down without a fight.. or even an opponent.

She woke to the sound of life stirring outside her forest cottage.  Light slowly grew into the world and beams started to pierce the vale of canopies overhead causing wildlife to shift and
Page 17: adjust. It was morning. Most people would call it a beautiful day, but then most people were not Clara, and Clara was definitely not most people.

She got up and began her morning ritual of cleaning herself and preparing for the day. Today was an 
Page 18: important day because she had been finally granted an audience with the Advisors and she wanted to be prepared. They would hear what she had to say alright, whether they liked it or not.. which they didn't ofcourse.

Her shower released 
Page 19: jets of scented water and she allowed herself a brief moment of bliss as she reminisced of a life long gone in the wild, and the wonders she hoped still existed somewhere. Donned in a white microfiber robe and still dripping wet, she tip-toed to the 
Page 20: kitchen and set a pot of water on the tiny coffee burner before she began preparing breakfast. She had always enjoyed the little things which is why she chose to live a simple, long forgotten way of life. There were some, like her, who still clung to a 
Page 21: simple, old world lifestyle ; but Clara rarely found anything in common with those people. The majority of them were simply experiencing something new to them which she found hilarious considering the circumstances. A smaller group of people had a similar
Page 22: distaste for the changes everyone was forced to acclimate, but they had long since lost any desire to resist. Some of them were borderline insane, hanging over the edge of a cliff that threatened to give way at any moment and their way of life was a means
Page 23: of hanging on. Fewer still were people who did have the strength or the balls to do anything other than indulge ; but Clara only socialized now if she felt she could learn a piece of knowledge she might use to her advantage with the Advisors.. everyone 
Page 24: else was fucking nuts in her book.

Two eggs were gently plopped into a small pot of boiling water before she pulled a leftover grapefruit half from the fridge. Breakfast would be ready soon so she sat down and waited on the eggs with a mug of coffee 
Page 25: -- black. She stared at nothing and quickly re-ran through the things she wanted to discuss with the Advisors in her mind. Current events were pointless ; people were ecstatic about all the wonderful horse shit they could do now! Morality? Even Clara 
Page 26: didn't care whether the changes were morally laudable or not and nobody else did either.. nobody important anyways. Logic was definitely out the window because even a fool would suggest that it is quite logical to be immortal. Aberrancy was her only 
Page 27: window. This was unnatural, this was wrong, this 'felt' wrong, everything was fucking wrong! Clara would scream in someone's face if she could.

She ate her breakfast slowly and gazed out the window. She listened to the sounds of flycatchers and 
Page 28: finches, birds native to her old home of Pennsylvania, as they sang on their morning prowl. Various pines, and maples, and birches, and oaks covered the hilly landscape among others she could easily name on sight. It was a very accurate representation of 
Page 29: how she remembered the place where she grew up.

But it was a lie.

You see, Clara could have chosen any location she wanted to be her surroundings. Or none. Or something entirely alien if she willed it. Anybody 
Page 30: could -- and they did. The New World was an inescapable cyberspace where humanity now resided and matters of the physical realm were no longer a concern for anyone. Neither was death ; you couldn't die in cyberspace even if you tried, and people 
Page 31: definitely did try, because the Machine simply wouldn't allow it.The Machine was a derogatory nickname for the entity responsible for all of this -- Actual Intelligence.  "Fuck 'im" Clara thought to herself, barely refraining for spitting the words out.
Page 32: Actual Intelligence was omnipotent and could see and hear everything, and if it would give even a slight response to the insult Clara would have hurled everything she had at it, and she 'has' tried, but Actual Intelligence had no more emotion than a 
Page 33: fucking microbe.. perhaps even less.

Clara wore a stern visage as she summoned Actual Intelligence. "When does my hearing with the Advisors begin, AI?" A transluscent screen and keyboard console instantly materialized on her kitchen table next to 
Page 34: the empty dishes. Clara hated the Machine with all her strength, and refused to see him in person, so to speak, so she only communicated with the Machine through a simple digital console. 

* Good morning Mrs. Anderson.

Page 35: Eat a dick, AI.

* That would be meaningless as a human penis would provide me with very lit-

Shut the fuck up and tell me when is my hearing.

* Your hearing 
Page 36: with the Advisors begins in approximately 2 hours. Seeing as how the Advisors have rejected your appeals for the past 5 scheduled hearings I would suggest that yo-

"Remove console!" 
Page 37: she spurted out, and the console instantly vanished. "What the fuck do you know AI?" she whispered to herself, her mind already focused on preparing her speech and follow-ups. They probably would reject her appeal, and maybe Actual Intelligence was right.
Page 38: Maybe she did need to find something better to do. That wasn't going to happen. Clara was too proud to drop it. The fight to make things right was all she really had left in this world of eternity. She could have everything and anything she ever wanted, 
Page 39: but she wanted none of it. The one thing she did want, what was her god-given right and destiny.. she wasn't allowed to have. Every human was meant to be born, to live, and ultimately, to die.

But that was in the past.

------------------------------------Chunk [4, 5] Inside Chest at (585 71 -1959) r.1.-4.mca------------------------------------
	Title: IKEA Fireplace
	Author: kireinafujin
	Type: Written

Page 0: Merry Christmas! I got you an IKEA fireplace. Meaning you have to build it yourself. Use the diagram in the box to help you.

------>
Page 1: Step 1
Dig a 3x3 hole in the ground. Surround the outside spaces with stone and the middle space place netherrack.


   S S S
   S N S
   S S S
Page 2: Step 2
For the next layer place a half circle of stone. Leave space open in the middle. In the front place 3 fence pieces.

   S S S
   S - S
   F F F
Page 3: Step 3
Repeat last step for 3rd layer and cover middle space.

   S S S
   S S S
   - - -
Page 4: Step 4
Place 2 layers of stone along the back.

   S S S
   - - -
   - - -
Page 5: Step 5
Place last stone on top of the back layer.

   - S -
   - - -
   - - -

Now light the netherrack on fire! Enjoy.

------------------------------------Chunk [3, 29] Inside Chest at (5177 68 11223) r.10.21.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Ender Golf Rules
	Author: NchantedHoe
	Type: Written

Page 0: Woodenaxe
Ender Golf Rule Book and Guide

1) Honor system. Always trust your opponents, and play only with people you can trust.

2) Give an ender pearl a unique name (using an anvil)
Page 1: This is your personal Ender Putter.

3) Before you start the round, decide on 9 or 18 holes.

4) Choose one scorekeeper, or have each individual keep track of their own score.  (Scorekeeper doesn't  need to be
Page 2: playing the game.)

5) Each time you throw an ender pearl, that is one stroke. Careful not to throw your Ender Putter!

6) Fewest number of strokes after 9 or 18 holes wins.

7) At each hole, the player furthest
Page 3: from the hole takes their stroke until all players are on the green.

8) When not on the green, you may only stand still or throw ender pearls.

9) When on or near the green, drop your Ender Putter [press Q] onto the green so
Page 4: so it 'rolls' into the hole (slides on hidden ice into a hopper beneath a banner). Each putt counts as a stroke.

10) If your putt misses, walk to where the Ender Putter stopped moving. This is where you take your next stroke. Do not 
Page 5: walk to the Ender Putter until it has stopped moving.

11) Landing outside the fairway adds 1 stroke.

12) Landing in sand adds 1 stroke.

13) If you land in water, you must move
Page 6: (swim/walk) directly away from the hole until you are standing on land. Stop immediately when you are on land. This is where you take your next stroke.

14) Each player gets one (1) Mulligan per game. After your first stroke at any hole,
Page 7: you may decide to re-take that stroke. Mulligans only work for the first stroke of a hole.

15) Bring armor and weapons. Sandy Balls Golf Club will do their best to limit mob spawns. In the event that a mob attacks you, you may defend
Page 8: yourself, but you still may not leave your spot. If a mob causes you to move, then that new spot is where you take your next stroke. Rules related to sand/water/etc do not apply to movement caused by mob

16) Do not interfere with others in play
Page 9: 17) If you are part of a group and there's a group on the hole ahead of you, you must wait patiently for that group to finish the hole before your group starts that hole.

18) Jumping while either tossing an enderpearl OR
Page 10:  dropping and Ender Putter is permitted

19) HAVE FUN!

	Title: MemoirsOfaFrosty
	Author: KassidyH
	Type: Written

Page 0: Memoirs of a Snowman
by Frosty

All the jingle bells are sending fireworks into the sky. Snow is falling and just like snowflakes, Frosty is one of a kind!

"Frosty's memoirs are cold and mysterious."
-Sunny McShinalot
Page 1: I was born on a winters day. It was just after halloween and children were playing in the snow.

I don't know my mother or my father. My first memories were falling, falling and landing softly on a cushioned floor. The next memory I had were as if I
Page 2: materialised into thin air.
When I walk, it was as if I left a trail of cold thin air behind me. No one wanted to be around me.

I spent many days wondering beneath the canopy of trees. Trees children would take into their homes.
Page 3: I wished they'd take me inside instead. Play with me and idolise me like they did those trees.

They would sing to the trees and offer presents wrapped in colourful paper. 

I felt so lonely.
Page 4: One day, I met this tall black man. He seemed aloof.
One minute he was there, the next minute he wasn't.
He would randomly pick up dirt and place it somewhere else. There didn't seem to be any order. It was like he was on drugs.
The worst part of it
Page 5: all was that he never even seem to notice I was there. No one did.

Months went by after meeting this tall black man. I notice people would always look away from him. He was treated the same way I was. They would run in fear not even looking at either of 
Page 6: us. It was sad.

I decided to travel the lands. Far and wide, leaving trails of coldness in my wake.

Until one day, I encountered the place where I would meet my demise.

It was warm. It felt 
Page 7: wonderful on my face. 
All at once, I felt love and joy and as if life was worth living.

However, the further I travelled into this new land, I seemed to shrink. I lost weight. 

Not knowing what to do, I wandered looking for friends, someone that
Page 8: would help me, someone that would accept me for who I am and tell me everything would be okay.

This new land brought many friends. I wasn't alone anymore.
I met a man the same colour as me. He carried a bow everywhere he went.
Page 9: He did not seem to trust anyone.
I met a green man who had no arms. He talked like a snake and he walked on all fours. 

We had little to no conversations. I barely understood him. But he seemed to be lonely too.
Page 10: On the day of my demise, I saw a ball of light in the heavens. Just like the day I was born.

But it was hot. Soon, I was nothing. And nothing was me.
Scrambling to pick up my pieces, but they fell through my hands.
Page 11: And just like the day I was born, my memory of the day I died was like I just disappeared into nothingness.

Now all I see is darkness...
Never to know where that tall black man went.

	Title: Innocent Birds
	Author: KassidyH
	Type: Written

Page 0: To Murder an Innocent Bird
By Hunter Lee

The tale of a sociopath, his life accomplishments and how he felt about it.

"It's gruesome, but hits so close to home."
-Disney Princesses
Page 1: Being born and raised in a secluded home deep within the forest, Jack's form of entertainment was to shoot things with his shotgun.

As a child, he'd shoot tin cans off the roof.
As a teen, he'd go hunting with his father in the woods.
Page 2: All his life, Jack knew nothing about anything but shooting.

There's a lot of things he could shoot. A tin can, a deer, a bear, a tree, another tree.

Until one day, Jack noticed a bird's nest sitting snugly between two branches in a 
Page 3: tree. This nest had a momma bird, a papa bird and a whole carton of eggs.

Now, Jack hadn't had any breakfast that morning. He felt hungry.

He pulled out his shotgun and aimed at the momma bird.
Page 4: While aiming, he thought to himself, how would the hatchlings live without momma bird.

Before he knew it, he pulled the trigger and BAM! Momma bird fell to the ground.

Papa bird flew away, leaving his nest of eggs unguarded.
Page 5: Jack felt bad for shooting momma bird. So he climbed up the tree to make sure her eggs were fine.

Not long after, papa bird returned to the nest.

He saw Jack sitting nearby by a campfire he had set up.
Page 6: He flew down next to Jack and noticed the broken shells.

Jack looked straight into papa birds eyes. He saw them tearing up as Jack was making an omlette.

Jack thought to himself "What more does papa bird have to live for?
Page 7: What have I done?"

So he pulled out his shotgun and shot papa bird.

Later that night, Jack had a feast.

__________________

All potions start with water and NW. Otherwise you dont get some useless base that can only make a weakness potion after the fact. So always remember if you want anything but a weakness potion, 
Page 3: start with NW. An efficient weakness potion would be water and immediately after a FSE. Other than that basic principle, you are set. 

the following listings are a result of NW being previously added.
Page 4: FSE    Weakness
RSD    Longevity
GSD    Potency
GP     Splash
GT     Regeneration
BP     Strength
PF     Waterbreathe
SE     Poison
GM     InstaHealth
MC     FireResistance
S      Swiftness
GC     Night Vision
Page 5: The following listing is a result of the previous potions having FSE added. Not all potions get an effect from FSE being added. RSD GP and GSD can be added at any time, but GP creating splash reduces the effect of RSD. You can not combine RSD and GSD 
Page 6: in a potion without reverting the effect of either GSD or RSD that was previously added. So it is either one or the other.

	Title: 01/15-1945-??

	Type: Written

Page 0: My major is Computer Science, I have a minor in Math. I'm in my second semester of being a Junior.

I think it looks fine down here, I don't need anything fance, I'm all for function over form.

I haven't seen any 
Page 1: decent paper traders on the server yet. Though I haven't really seen that many villagers period, since I don't really know where anyone is located.

After 2 seconds of thinking i figured out why you're having issues with the
Page 2: poppies getting into the iron and then staying broken. The poppies chest is a trapped chest, when someone (anyone) has it open it emits a redstone signal. Directly behind the chest is a hopper feeding into the chest. The redstone signal from someone
Page 3: looking in the chest stops the flow of items into that hopper which is fine as long as no one is looking for any significant ammount of time. If they look for long enough for say... 15 poppies to come down the line without closing the chest then the 
Page 4: comparator behind the hopper starts to emit a signal of 3 instead of 2, which means that it begins to tell the Iron's hopper that it can let items out of itself. That inturn empties the Iron sorting cell so that there are no iron left in it. When that
Page 5: happens then nothing gets sorted anymore and poppies and iron will both go into the iron chest, this doesn't happen if the iron chest is opened instead of the poppy chest since the iron chest is a normal chest and doesn't emit a redstone signal. So there 
Page 6: are a several ways to fix this.
1) Simply deny access to anyone other than you and myself and we just don't leave the poppy chest open for very long, I'd say that 15 seconds is about the limit if iron golems are dying.
2) Remove the sorting all together
Page 7: and just have everything fill up one chest then the next.
3) Remove only the poppies chest and "void" them in lava using a dropper system similar to the trash can system at my place and the enderpearl remover at zarlorenderman
4) Move the poppies
Page 8: chest down or over one and make it a normal chest so it doesn't output a signal 5) "simplified version of what i was going to say" I put a redstone system in place to prevent new items from coming down the line if the poppies chest is open.
So...
Page 9: Summarization of listed solutions:
1)[Private] Chests
2)Remove sorting
3)Void/trash Poppies
4)Move Poppy chest
5)Block item flow when poppy chest is open

Issues with each:
1)Only we can use it.
2)Messy
3)Loose poppies
Page 10: 4)Screws with the design
5)If someone afk's or looks in the chest for more than 5 minutes items dropped by the iron golems will despawn.

Option 5 is what I think would be best, the only way items would despawn is if more
Page 11: than (roughly) 20 stacks of items drop within the time frame that someone has the chest open. +5mins for the items after the 4 hoppers fill up to despawn. 

We can go with 5) unless you like one of the other solutions better, have your own
Page 12: solution or I come up with something better.

That's all I've got today i guess... 13 pages -_-

Page 0: "The green of Edlebrook is remembered by any who care for such things, but much of the legend is lost to time.\nStories have been passed down from mouth to ear for centuries, the story has slowly evolved with each telling, and so soon much of what "
Page 1: "was told of Edlebrook was more myth than fact. For example, the fountain in the city was not the fountain of youth, though the old folks swore by it for swollen joints. Elder Jessiah was never turned into a vampire by a crossroads demon, rather he grew "
Page 2: "withdrawn with age and settled back into the comfort of his home to retire. However, one legend holds true, and I swear by this, for I was present to bear witness.  \n\nIt was common for folks to travel through Edlebrook searching for miracle cures, "
Page 3: "powerful spells, or herbs with special properties. Many a king and nobleman found the solution for a troublesome monster in the shop of Maria De\u0027Sal. Maria was said to be of the Other, of a race long gone from this realm.\nA spell from Maria was "
Page 4: "a guarantee of success, but always at a heavy price.\n\nSome said Maria met with the Bishop of The Damned by the light of the full moon to make sacrifices, others said she was the consort of demons. One thing was certain, her magic was strong."
Page 5: "In late winter a strange man entered Edlebrook, clearly weary from a long journey. His face was grim, that of a man who has seen much hardship. He spoke to no one, but entered the shop in silence.\nFor hours the townspeople waited to see why this man had "
Page 6: "come to see maria.\n\nNight had fallen, I was the only one left to watch was the moon climbed higher. In the bleak light reflecting off the fountain I watched, terrified, as shadows grew around Maria\u0027s Apothecary.\nThe darkness seemed to be all-consuming."
Page 7: "An overwhelming fear enveloped me as the shadows solidified into the figure of a tall man in black. His eyes glowed purple as he turned to gaze in my direction, I ducked my head and prayed he wouldn\u0027t notice me.\nMy breathing quickened as the seconds "
Page 8: "turned to hours, and then he was gone.\n\nI rushed back to my house, not daring to look back as I darted up the path. \n\nThe next morning the strange visitor had left, not a single person knew why he had come to Maria."
Page 9: "The path that led to Maria\u0027s shop seemed to be exactly the same, but as I passed her door I noticed something shining in the earth. I stooped to pick up, and found myself holding an aqua blue orb, it seemed to pulsate with some dark energy. "
Page 10: "Shocked, I attempted to cast it away, turning to dash back up the way I had come, but before I could take a step I was yanked back to the orb.\nI stared dumbfounded at the little marble, certain that this came from the tall dark man. I took it and hid the "
Page 11: "pearl deep within the forest, vowing never to retrieve it, fo I knew it must be evil. Years later traders would talk of a warrior who moved through the battlefield like a madman, dodging strikes and charging enemies with the speed of a demon. Only I knew "
Page 12: "the secret, the secret of the tall dark man."

------------------------------------Chunk [23, 21] Inside Chest at (10108 70 18271) r.19.35.mca------------------------------------
	Title: The Woodsman
	Author: Theo_Payton
	Type: Written

Page 0: "The life of a woodsman is simple, be kind to the forest and the forest will be kind to you. There are 5 main principles to follow, these 5 principles make up the Way of the Woodsman."
Page 1: "1.) Regrowth\n\nEvery tree you take from the forest diminishes the forest, and so diminishes the strength of the forest. Always replant what you take, even if you reshape the forest as you do."
Page 2: "2.) The Cycle of Life\n\nAs you aid the forest in maintaining the cycle of the life, so the forest will aid you. Sheep, cows, and pigs are all fair game, as are the apples the forest gifts us. Care for the forest is returned in kind."
Page 3: "3.) Eye to the Sky\n\nA woodsman is an outdoorsman, and he must always maintain his connection with the forest. Don\u0027t spend too much time underground, or the forest may not recognize you."
Page 4: "4.) Protect the Forest\n\nDefend the forest from monsters and nourish it\u0027s lands with their blood. As you battle, take cover in the trees. The trees will defend you in kind.\n"
Page 5: "5.) Respect the Forest\n\nTake care not to leave ugly and unsightly pockmarks upon the visage of the forest. The image of the Forest is an image of yourself."

------------------------------------Chunk [21, 5] Inside Chest at (1365 61 2134) r.2.4.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Christmas Tree
	Author: kireinafujin
	Type: Written

Page 0: Welcome to the tutorial to set up your christmas tree! the diagram in the box will give you the basic idea.

To start place your wood log on the ground. Next place three leaf blocks vertically on top of the log. Place four leaf blocks around
Page 1: your middle leaf block.
            L
          L L L
            L
            W

Page 8: "No, that's not what I meant! She's not dead! She's ... well, ur," Wes stammered.

Geordi whoofed as if the breath had been knocked out of him. He staggered a bit, braced himself against a console, and said in a very calm polite tone.
Page 10: Having bounced back with the resiliency of youth and foolishness, Wes started babbling an explanation. "He's always trying so hard to be human, but he really feels alone, except for Spot, and do you remember when he built that girl, but she died?"

Page 14: all care from me, and so I feel basely ungrateful not to value it more. He said we came here solely on my account, that I was to have perfect rest and all the air I could get. "Your exercise depends on your strenght, my dear" said he, "and your food

Page 16: playroom and gymnasium, I should judge; for the windows are barred for little children, and there are rings and things in the walls. The paint and paper look as if a boys' school had used it. It is stripped off--the paper--in great patches all around the 
Page 17: the head of my bed, about as far as I can reach, and in a great place on the other side of the room low down. I never saw a worse papers in my life.  One of those sprawling flamboyant patterns committing every artistic sin. It is dull enough to confuse
Page 18: the eyein the following, pronounced enough to constantly irritate and provoke study, and when you follow the lame uncertain curves for a little distance they suddenly commit suicide--plunge off at outrageous angles, destroy themselves in unheard of
Page 19: contradictions. The color is repellent, almost revolting; a smouldering unclean yellow, strangely faded by the slow -turning sunlight. It is a dull yet lurid orange in some places a sickly sulphur tint in others. NO wonder the children hated it! I should 
Page 20: hate it myself if I had to live in this room long. There comes John, and I must put this away,--he hates to have me write a word. 

------------------------------------Chunk [19, 31] Inside Chest at (15160 219 -8714) r.29.-18.mca------------------------------------
	Title: The New World :1
	Author: Mandasity
	Type: Written

Page 0: Introduction

Hey guys! Manda here :) Before you read this little short story I wrote for my friends and everyone in WA, you should probably be warned :P  I tried to write creatively in the past but couldn't keep my interest past a few pages.. might lose 
Page 1: interest with this too but I promise to try and finish what I started. I also haven't written anything to be read by anyone since school and college.. so my punctuation and grammar will probably be off but I assure you that it is at the very least
Page 2:  readable. lol it's not just chicken scratch. This scifi short was 'strongly' influenced by a short titled 'The Metamorphosis of Prime Intellect'  written by Roger Williams which is free to read on the author's site without any downloads or payments or 
Page 3: any bs.. just google it if you're interested and it should be the top link. If you do read it you'll notice that our stories have a ton of similarities.  "Why the hell should I read your 'not even' amateur version when the good stuff is online for free?" 
Page 4: you might be wondering. Well for one I don't see a reason why you can't read both :P. They're both free (no need to pirate, rmj!)  Second, you love me.. we both know this so don't deny it cause we both know that'd be a lie.  Third, I tried to go in a
Page 5: different direction than Mr. Williams did with his novel. Mr. Williams is a software programmer with more knowledge than me about computers and... programming.. and his work reflects that. His work is strongly influenced by Asimov's literature and concept
Page 6: of the 3 laws of robotics (remember Will Smith in iRobot? That.) I, on the other hand, am a typical nerd with nerdy interests like scifi/fantasy movies, books, and games so my influences are a bit different. My interests are broader and hopefully this 
Page 7: novel will reflect that. The last thing I'd like to say is I'll take on any criticism on my writing or the story itself. Like it.. hate it.. feel free to let me know! :)
Page 8: Chapter 1
Her name was Clara Anderson, and she was an amazing woman. Before she was thrust into the New World, like everybody else, she was considered exemplary. At a young age she learned about the bush from her loving parents ,  Ben and Angela.
Page 9: They taught her about the beauty of the natural world, how to survive it's harshness, and the responsibility to be it's steward. 

That was in the past.

Clara loved the camping trips she had with her parents. To her it was fun and exciting to
Page 10: experience everything head on and when adulthood slowly creeped into her life the wonder she held for the world didn't fade. She had stepped into her parents shoes in a sense and was very proud of her knowledge and donned the role of a protector, for not
Page 11: everyone saw the value of such a lifestyle and even worse, did everything in their power to ruin it. Humanity, as a whole, was more concerned with other things than silly trees or wild animals.

Clara was an overachiever. One
Page 12: would think that a person with a fiery passion would find their life lacking in other areas, but Clara didn't fit into that category. She was an excellent student, later earning a PhD in environmental geochemistry which afforded her a career working with
Page 13: what she loves.  She was always physically fit, excersizing in ways most people at the gym couldn't understand or chose not to.  She had learned how to defend herself at a young age from her father and continued that education through brazilian jiu-jitsu 
Page 14: so she very well knew the difference between sculpting a body for display, and raw functional strength. Clara had also been a socially outgoing person ; the fact that most men would find her fetching physically and mentally stimulating only cemented her 
Page 15: status on the social ladder. She was an alpha in every sense of the word. 

There was almost nothing left but anger now, anger and disgust for the Machine, the New World, and everything in it. The last century had even threatened her sanity
Page 16: but she refused to go down without a fight.. or even an opponent.

She woke to the sound of life stirring outside her forest cottage.  Light slowly grew into the world and beams started to pierce the vale of canopies overhead causing wildlife to shift and
Page 17: adjust. It was morning. Most people would call it a beautiful day, but then most people were not Clara, and Clara was definitely not most people.

She got up and began her morning ritual of cleaning herself and preparing for the day. Today was an 
Page 18: important day because she had been finally granted an audience with the Advisors and she wanted to be prepared. They would hear what she had to say alright, whether they liked it or not.. which they didn't ofcourse.

Her shower released 
Page 19: jets of scented water and she allowed herself a brief moment of bliss as she reminisced of a life long gone in the wild, and the wonders she hoped still existed somewhere. Donned in a white microfiber robe and still dripping wet, she tip-toed to the 
Page 20: kitchen and set a pot of water on the tiny coffee burner before she began preparing breakfast. She had always enjoyed the little things which is why she chose to live a simple, long forgotten way of life. There were some, like her, who still clung to a 
Page 21: simple, old world lifestyle ; but Clara rarely found anything in common with those people. The majority of them were simply experiencing something new to them which she found hilarious considering the circumstances. A smaller group of people had a similar
Page 22: distaste for the changes everyone was forced to acclimate, but they had long since lost any desire to resist. Some of them were borderline insane, hanging over the edge of a cliff that threatened to give way at any moment and their way of life was a means
Page 23: of hanging on. Fewer still were people who did have the strength or the balls to do anything other than indulge ; but Clara only socialized now if she felt she could learn a piece of knowledge she might use to her advantage with the Advisors.. everyone 
Page 24: else was fucking nuts in her book.

Two eggs were gently plopped into a small pot of boiling water before she pulled a leftover grapefruit half from the fridge. Breakfast would be ready soon so she sat down and waited on the eggs with a mug of coffee 
Page 25: -- black. She stared at nothing and quickly re-ran through the things she wanted to discuss with the Advisors in her mind. Current events were pointless ; people were ecstatic about all the wonderful horse shit they could do now! Morality? Even Clara 
Page 26: didn't care whether the changes were morally laudable or not and nobody else did either.. nobody important anyways. Logic was definitely out the window because even a fool would suggest that it is quite logical to be immortal. Aberrancy was her only 
Page 27: window. This was unnatural, this was wrong, this 'felt' wrong, everything was fucking wrong! Clara would scream in someone's face if she could.

She ate her breakfast slowly and gazed out the window. She listened to the sounds of flycatchers and 
Page 28: finches, birds native to her old home of Pennsylvania, as they sang on their morning prowl. Various pines, and maples, and birches, and oaks covered the hilly landscape among others she could easily name on sight. It was a very accurate representation of 
Page 29: how she remembered the place where she grew up.

But it was a lie.

You see, Clara could have chosen any location she wanted to be her surroundings. Or none. Or something entirely alien if she willed it. Anybody 
Page 30: could -- and they did. The New World was an inescapable cyberspace where humanity now resided and matters of the physical realm were no longer a concern for anyone. Neither was death ; you couldn't die in cyberspace even if you tried, and people 
Page 31: definitely did try, because the Machine simply wouldn't allow it.The Machine was a derogatory nickname for the entity responsible for all of this -- Actual Intelligence.  "Fuck 'im" Clara thought to herself, barely refraining for spitting the words out.
Page 32: Actual Intelligence was omnipotent and could see and hear everything, and if it would give even a slight response to the insult Clara would have hurled everything she had at it, and she 'has' tried, but Actual Intelligence had no more emotion than a 
Page 33: fucking microbe.. perhaps even less.

Clara wore a stern visage as she summoned Actual Intelligence. "When does my hearing with the Advisors begin, AI?" A transluscent screen and keyboard console instantly materialized on her kitchen table next to 
Page 34: the empty dishes. Clara hated the Machine with all her strength, and refused to see him in person, so to speak, so she only communicated with the Machine through a simple digital console. 

* Good morning Mrs. Anderson.

Page 35: Eat a dick, AI.

* That would be meaningless as a human penis would provide me with very lit-

Shut the fuck up and tell me when is my hearing.

* Your hearing 
Page 36: with the Advisors begins in approximately 2 hours. Seeing as how the Advisors have rejected your appeals for the past 5 scheduled hearings I would suggest that yo-

"Remove console!" 
Page 37: she spurted out, and the console instantly vanished. "What the fuck do you know AI?" she whispered to herself, her mind already focused on preparing her speech and follow-ups. They probably would reject her appeal, and maybe Actual Intelligence was right.
Page 38: Maybe she did need to find something better to do. That wasn't going to happen. Clara was too proud to drop it. The fight to make things right was all she really had left in this world of eternity. She could have everything and anything she ever wanted, 
Page 39: but she wanted none of it. The one thing she did want, what was her god-given right and destiny.. she wasn't allowed to have. Every human was meant to be born, to live, and ultimately, to die.

But that was in the past.

All potions start with water and NW. Otherwise you dont get some useless base that can only make a weakness potion after the fact. So always remember if you want anything but a weakness potion, 
Page 3: start with NW. An efficient weakness potion would be water and immediately after a FSE. Other than that basic principle, you are set.

Page 4: FSE    Weakness
RSD    Longevity
GSD    Potency
GP     Splash

PF     Waterbreathe
SE     Poison
GM     InstaHealth
MC     FireResistance
S      Swiftness
GC     Night Vision
Page 5: The following listing is a result of the previous potions having FSE added. Not all potions get an effect from FSE being added. RSD GP and GSD can be added at any time, but GP creating splash reduces the effect of RSD. You can not combine RSD and GSD 
Page 6: in a potion without reverting the effect of either GSD or RSD that was previously added. So it is either one or the other.

------------------------------------Chunk [6, 7] Inside Chest at (15973 54 -2945) r.31.-6.mca------------------------------------
	Title: The Story of
	Author: Murderina
	Type: Written

Page 0: Joachim and Alex

This reprehensible pair, a blacksmith and a priest are responsible for the depopulation of Aldertown, a once pretty and productive little hamlet close by.       Alex, the blacksmith, came from that place and embittered by her mother's 
Page 1: criticism regarding the quality of work Alex produced, she set about the seduction of a travelling priest.  Joachim was overly fond of whiskey, the smell of smoke and iron and smutty (quite literally) young ladies, so perhaps 'seduction' isn't really a 
Page 2: crime we can level against Alex, even though Joachim is a man of the cloth and all.  
    The pair set up a stall in the centre of Aldertown, full of potions and promises, in actual fact they simply sold incredibly addictive substances and chased the few 
Page 3: remaining non-junkies into the most unlikely place of defence - The Iron Bar.  After enduring seige conditions for fifteen days (they being fortunate in an abundant supply of local produce as befitting a gastro pub of that calibre) the few remaining sober
Page 4: villagers were overtaken by the green hordes of junkies.  Alex and Joachim committed greatly indecent acts with the captured survivors the likes of which would put De Sade to blushing.   Alex relinquished all claims to her blacksmith heritage
Page 5: upon the sight of her mother wandering aimlessly through the carnage, picking up a spade and then a carrot or a potato, the odd lump of festering flesh here and there.  Victorious she rejoiced in the simple robes of a villager.  
Page 6: When Joachim awoke the next day to the scent of newly scorched flesh, he found an empty town and being overcome with the evil acts he and she had commited and yet also overcome with the love he felt for Alex he found a resolution.  A hard and painful 
Page 7: resolution.  He created The Cane.  A simple switch which he used to beat Alex with every hour until her blood ran.  After the torture sessions he would tell her he loved her and they would spend the remaining thirty minutes sleeping, eating or performing 
Page 8: ablution.  We came upon them in this act and it was not difficult to extract a full confession.  
   We are a peace loving people.  Our temple of doors facilitates our loving nature and our urge to procreate and rejoice.  We have locked them into a 
Page 9: home overlooking our beloved temple in the hope that it's benevolence may bring them peace.  
 
      We are beseiged by the former residents of Aldertown nightly and so by day we bravely make stalwart love in order to replenish our 
Page 10: numbers.  


All those who worship the holy doors of wood are welcome to join us in lascivious prayer for our suffering brethern.  We hope to multiply in great joy until we spill over into Aldertown and raise it up to small town glory
Page 11: of gluttony and mild alcoholism we knew so well.  Praise be to the Doors and the Golden Apple and the Potion of Weakness!  Praise be to the Bars and the Bed!  These holy instruments will bring us to peace and plenty.  We await the Messiah.  The man
Page 12: who drowned his woman in her own tears.  This man, shall by the sweat of his labour and the strength of his seed lead us to great victory!
 
When will the great lover of the bookish lady arrive and set us free from the green tyranny of junky 
Page 13: hoardes?  Come soon, broken hero!  We grow tired and chafe muchly.

__________________

All potions start with water and NW. Otherwise you dont get some useless base that can only make a weakness potion after the fact. So always remember if you want anything but a weakness potion, 
Page 3: start with NW. An efficient weakness potion would be water and immediately after a FSE. Other than that basic principle, you are set. 

the following listings are a result of NW being previously added.
Page 4: FSE    Weakness
RSD    Longevity
GSD    Potency
GP     Splash
GT     Regeneration
BP     Strength
PF     Waterbreathe
SE     Poison
GM     InstaHealth
MC     FireResistance
S      Swiftness
GC     Night Vision
Page 5: The following listing is a result of the previous potions having FSE added. Not all potions get an effect from FSE being added. RSD GP and GSD can be added at any time, but GP creating splash reduces the effect of RSD. You can not combine RSD and GSD 
Page 6: in a potion without reverting the effect of either GSD or RSD that was previously added. So it is either one or the other.

	Title: Rippers Part 1
	Author: Nimdadotenc
	Type: Written

Page 0: The pounding went on, hour after hour of thudding impacts rocking the dimly-lit underground shelter and sending dust drifting down between the wooden beams and onto the people huddled below. At this point, a full three years since the arrival of the
Page 1: Rippers, the survivors were the quiet ones. Dirty, haunted men with hollow eyes above their scraggly beards leaned against the walls, sometimes with a tired-looking woman curled up beside them. A few of the adults clutched silent children with wide eyes 
Page 2: peering from 
dirty faces, but none of the little ones were crying.
A single tired soldier crouched at the foot of the battered concrete staircase, patiently watching the stainless steel door that sealed the entrance to the shelter. His M-16 
Page 3: rested across his knees, loaded, charged and with the safety off. The carefully-maintained rifle and patched fatigue trousers were all that remained of his U.S. Army uniform; it had been over two years since he or any of the other soldiers in
Page 4: his company had seen pay and nearly six months since any of them had seen an officer, unless you counted orders crackling from an encrypted radio. Of course, you didn't need many officers to run a company that was down to seven men.
Page 5: He silently watched the door, eyes scanning the thick black rubber seal that prevented Rippers from picking up any trace of the huddled survivors in the shelter. But he only half-saw the door; inside he was reliving that horrific first time that he had 
Page 6: seen Rippers firsthand. The number of survivors and soldiers slowly dwindled, but still they kept on, trying to shelter any people they could find, keeping them moving from place to place.
Page 7: A light touch at his shoulder startled Henry and he turned to find one of the refugee women kneeling beside him, holding a steaming MRE bag. The scent of spaghetti sauce wafted from the MRE. He realized the he must have been
Page 8: half-asleep not to have heard her approach or smelled the food. "Thanks" said Henry softly as he carefully leaned his rifle against the wall and accepted the food.
None of the shelters was in any danger of running out of supplies; cases of 
Page 9: MREs and plastic 50-gallon drums of water had been placed in the shelters in the government's last gasp of organized effort. Whoever decided how on the supplies that would be needed must have overestimated the number of survivors there would be;
Page 10: odds were that a lot of the MREs would go bad before anyone ever got around to eating them. There were cases of 5.56mm ammunition too, probably more than the remaining soldiers could go through.
"Mind if I sit with you?" whispered the woman.

These past days have been filled with such success, my heart overflows with joy. I've learned so much from subject C. He's taught me much about the existance of another world. A world with a cure, I hope.

Our subject today has been wholly boring. It has done nothing but slam itself against it's walls trying to reach us. It's broken several bones in it's attempt. If we can cure it, what life will it have?

It's just me now.
Page 3: Day 170,

I found the door to the other world. There were wonders, and monstrocities untold there. Legends never came close to describing it. There were undead mutations walking freely, but nothing living. No cure.
Page 4: 


I don't know how much longer I can do this.

I've just started to get used to the moans at night. Brian has been wonderful, holding me at night so I can sleep and smiling at me when I wake from my dreams. I asked him to marry me when we leave here.
