------------------------------------Chunk [12, 12] Inside Chest at (4301 56 6855) r.8.13.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Potions Guide
	Author: flame_chick
	Type: Written

Page 0: Potions Guide

Add nether wart to water bottles to make an awkward potion. All recipes (except weakness) require this to start.

Single ingredients

Rabbit's Foot - Potion of Leaping *R *G
Page 1: Magma Cream - Potion of Fire Resistance *R
Sugar - Potion of Swiftness *R *G
Pufferfish - Potion of Water Breathing *R
Glistering Melon - Potion of Healing *G
Spider Eye - Potion of Poison *R *G
Golden Carrot - Potion of Night Vision *R

Page 2: Ghast Tear - Potion of Regeneration *R *G
Blaze Powder - Potion of Strength *R *G
Fermented Spider Eye - Potion of Weakness

2nd ingredient potions

To make....
Potion of Slowness
add FSE (fermented spider eye) to Potion of Leaping, Fire Resis
Page 3: or swiftness.

Potion of Harming - Add FSE to potion of water breathing, healing, or poison.

Potion of Invisibility - Add FSE to potion of night vision.

cont  -->
Page 4: notes

*R - can add redstone dust to noted potions to make it last longer.

*G - can add glowstone dust to noted potions to make it stronger.


Page 5: Hope this helps :)

This book took many tries, and fails, but its finally DONE.. I hope

take care.. bye bye

[GSD] for *II*

------------------------------------Chunk [21, 30] Inside Chest at (43347 63 -1556) r.84.-4.mca------------------------------------
	Title: MemoirsOfaFrosty
	Author: KassidyH
	Type: Written

Page 0: Memoirs of a Snowman
by Frosty

All the jingle bells are sending fireworks into the sky. Snow is falling and just like snowflakes, Frosty is one of a kind!

"Frosty's memoirs are cold and mysterious."
-Sunny McShinalot
Page 1: I was born on a winters day. It was just after halloween and children were playing in the snow.

I don't know my mother or my father. My first memories were falling, falling and landing softly on a cushioned floor. The next memory I had were as if I
Page 2: materialised into thin air.
When I walk, it was as if I left a trail of cold thin air behind me. No one wanted to be around me.

I spent many days wondering beneath the canopy of trees. Trees children would take into their homes.
Page 3: I wished they'd take me inside instead. Play with me and idolise me like they did those trees.

They would sing to the trees and offer presents wrapped in colourful paper. 

I felt so lonely.
Page 4: One day, I met this tall black man. He seemed aloof.
One minute he was there, the next minute he wasn't.
He would randomly pick up dirt and place it somewhere else. There didn't seem to be any order. It was like he was on drugs.
The worst part of it
Page 5: all was that he never even seem to notice I was there. No one did.

Months went by after meeting this tall black man. I notice people would always look away from him. He was treated the same way I was. They would run in fear not even looking at either of 
Page 6: us. It was sad.

I decided to travel the lands. Far and wide, leaving trails of coldness in my wake.

Until one day, I encountered the place where I would meet my demise.

It was warm. It felt 
Page 7: wonderful on my face. 
All at once, I felt love and joy and as if life was worth living.

However, the further I travelled into this new land, I seemed to shrink. I lost weight. 

Not knowing what to do, I wandered looking for friends, someone that
Page 8: would help me, someone that would accept me for who I am and tell me everything would be okay.

This new land brought many friends. I wasn't alone anymore.
I met a man the same colour as me. He carried a bow everywhere he went.
Page 9: He did not seem to trust anyone.
I met a green man who had no arms. He talked like a snake and he walked on all fours. 

We had little to no conversations. I barely understood him. But he seemed to be lonely too.
Page 10: On the day of my demise, I saw a ball of light in the heavens. Just like the day I was born.

But it was hot. Soon, I was nothing. And nothing was me.
Scrambling to pick up my pieces, but they fell through my hands.
Page 11: And just like the day I was born, my memory of the day I died was like I just disappeared into nothingness.

Now all I see is darkness...
Never to know where that tall black man went.



------------------------------------Chunk [21, 30] Inside Chest at (43345 63 -1556) r.84.-4.mca------------------------------------
	Title: Innocent Birds
	Author: KassidyH
	Type: Written

Page 0: To Murder an Innocent Bird
By Hunter Lee

The tale of a sociopath, his life accomplishments and how he felt about it.

"It's gruesome, but hits so close to home."
-Disney Princesses
Page 1: Being born and raised in a secluded home deep within the forest, Jack's form of entertainment was to shoot things with his shotgun.

As a child, he'd shoot tin cans off the roof.
As a teen, he'd go hunting with his father in the woods.
Page 2: All his life, Jack knew nothing about anything but shooting.

There's a lot of things he could shoot. A tin can, a deer, a bear, a tree, another tree.

Until one day, Jack noticed a bird's nest sitting snugly between two branches in a 
Page 3: tree. This nest had a momma bird, a papa bird and a whole carton of eggs.

Now, Jack hadn't had any breakfast that morning. He felt hungry.

He pulled out his shotgun and aimed at the momma bird.
Page 4: While aiming, he thought to himself, how would the hatchlings live without momma bird.

Before he knew it, he pulled the trigger and BAM! Momma bird fell to the ground.

Papa bird flew away, leaving his nest of eggs unguarded.
Page 5: Jack felt bad for shooting momma bird. So he climbed up the tree to make sure her eggs were fine.

Not long after, papa bird returned to the nest.

He saw Jack sitting nearby by a campfire he had set up.
Page 6: He flew down next to Jack and noticed the broken shells.

Jack looked straight into papa birds eyes. He saw them tearing up as Jack was making an omlette.

Jack thought to himself "What more does papa bird have to live for?
Page 7: What have I done?"

So he pulled out his shotgun and shot papa bird.

Later that night, Jack had a feast.

Page 0: WA Specific Rules;

DISCLAIMERS -
The lights on the di will not be even, if you want to fix it go ahead, but I'm too lazy.

You will have to press the di button (Nether brick) twice to simulate two dice rolls.

Page 1: IT WILL BE EXTREMELY EASY TO CHEAT IN THIS GAME. If you want to play, TRY to play with people you think would HOPEFULLY not cheat. Even though that will be pretty tough to do.

If items are stolen from the containers, I will try to eventually replace them
Page 2: Rules;

1. Pick your color and remove the wool from the chest. This will be used to show ownership, houses, and hotels. Place the wool between the iron pressure plates for each of these. 1=ownership, 2-5=houses, (cont'd)
Page 3: 2-high on middle=hotel.

2. Take one row of money from the money chest. (5 of $1,$5,$10 - 6 of $20 - 2 of $50,$100,$200).

3. Play like regular monopoly.

4. ????????
Page 4: 5, 3 rolls of doubles DO mean instant jail. 

6. Chance, Community Chest and GO all warrant ONE press of the buttons for an item. The special GO money blocks can be exchanged at the bank if desired.
Page 5: 7. The chest cart that goes around the board is for transferring money. Just flip the switch at the desired location and the cart will stop there. 

8. If I stop playing again and someone needs special perms, just post on the forums.
Page 6: Anything else, just ask/refer to original monopoly rules. 

Yes this may breed arguments and name-calling, but that is all in the aim of keeping the true heart of monopoly.

I guess that's it...
